● Fix found — the missing line is DECK_RECOGNITION_ENABLE=true

  There are two separate switches in Forge, and I only had you flip the wrong
  one:

  ┌──────────────────────────┬─────────────┬────────────────────────────────┐
  │          Switch          │   Default   │          What it does          │
  ├──────────────────────────┼─────────────┼────────────────────────────────┤
  │                          │ false ←     │ Master ON/OFF. When false,     │
  │ DECK_RECOGNITION_ENABLE  │ missing     │ Forge never contacts the       │
  │                          │             │ sidecar at all                 │
  ├──────────────────────────┼─────────────┼────────────────────────────────┤
  │                          │ false ← you │ Whether AI uses sidecar data   │
  │ SIDECAR_INFLUENCE_ENABLE │  set this   │ after it arrives. Useless      │
  │                          │             │ without the master switch      │
  └──────────────────────────┴─────────────┴────────────────────────────────┘

  You set the influence switch, but the master switch was still off, so Forge
  never made any of the POST /identify-own-archetype / /recognize calls.

  On your phone, edit Default.ai again

  Add this single line:
  DECK_RECOGNITION_ENABLE=true

  (The other SIDECAR_* lines you already added stay — they're still needed.)

  Final block should look like:
  DECK_RECOGNITION_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_INFLUENCE_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_ROLE_ASSESSMENT_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_HAND_VALUATION_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_OPPONENT_INFERENCE_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_TARGETING_ENABLE=true
  SIDECAR_MULLIGAN_ENABLE=true

  Faster way to test without editing the phone file

  DeckRecognitionFeature.isEnabled() also accepts a Java system property
  override. If you want to confirm the fix works without re-editing the phone
  file, you could pass -Dforge.ai.deckRecognition=true to the JVM — but on
  Android there's no easy way to add JVM args, so editing the profile is the
  right path.

  After you save the change and fully restart Forge, start a new game. The first
   thing you should see is POST /identify-own-archetype arrive in the sidecar
  log on game start, then a stream of POST /recognize calls as your opponent
  plays cards. Tell me when it's started and I'll watch the log live.

● Classic Android gotcha — cleartext HTTP blocked at the OS level. Java
  HttpURLConnection in an Android app needs explicit permission to make plain
  HTTP calls (non-HTTPS) since Android 9+. Browser calls (your dashboard view)
  bypass this. Let me verify.

● Confirmed — the manifest is missing android:usesCleartextTraffic="true". Since
   targetSdkVersion=35, Android blocks all plain-HTTP traffic from the app by
  default. INTERNET permission is there, but cleartext is denied. Browser polls
  work because they're a separate app with its own policy.

● Diagnosis confirmed and patched

  Root cause: Android 9+ blocks cleartext (plain HTTP) traffic from apps by
  default. Your manifest had targetSdkVersion=35 with no exemption, so Forge's
  Java HttpURLConnection was being silently denied at the OS layer — connections
   never reached the sidecar. The dashboard view worked because Chrome is a
  different app with its own policy.

  The proof from your log:
  - attach() ran correctly: enabled=true sysprop=true
  - /health check failed at attach: did not respond to /health
  - 4288 POST /recognize attempts, ALL returned empty Optional → silent
  IOExceptions logged at DEBUG (not visible in your log file)

  Patch applied (two files):
  1. forge-gui-android/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml — added
  android:networkSecurityConfig="@xml/network_security_config"
  2. forge-gui-android/res/xml/network_security_config.xml (new) — allows
  cleartext only to Tailscale IPs (your sidecar 100.110.52.69, plus loopback for
   testing). Everything else still requires HTTPS, preserving Android's default
  safety.

  Next steps

  cd /home/lou/Development/forge-1
  mvn -pl forge-gui-android -am -DskipTests package
  # install the new APK on your phone (adb / sideload)

  After install:
  - Open Forge → start a new constructed match against the AI
  - Watch the sidecar log (tail -F 
  /home/lou/Development/forge-1/forge-llm-sidecar/logs/sidecar.log)
  - You should immediately see POST /identify-own-archetype followed by POST 
  /recognize once the AI's opponent (you) plays a card

  If for some reason you still don't see traffic after this rebuild, the next
  thing to check is whether the sidecar's localhost resolution is somehow
  specific (we shouldn't have that issue since you're using a direct IP, but
  worth flagging).
